<div id="review_79138126" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/79138126" />
    <a title="Tori" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1676497-tori"><img alt="Tori" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487511451p2/1676497.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/79138126?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tori" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tori" href="/user/show/1676497-tori">Tori</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1676497-tori?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1676497-tori?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer79138126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2532738441505966262">Ok, I'm seriously done with this shit. Really. This series started GREAT! I loved it, but it all went downhill. Fast. I don't have time for this soul-mate, dramatic 'Fug', 'hel-lo', 'OMG', shit. And then we turn around and have a bunch of teenagers with special powers fucking up and apologizing and being forgiven when they really deserve to be smacked. ARGH, It's like House of Night all over again!<br/><br/>And I get why Damen has such a large vocabulary, he's a million years old, but what the fuck? Ever </span>
  <span id="freeText2532738441505966262" style="display:none">Ok, I'm seriously done with this shit. Really. This series started GREAT! I loved it, but it all went downhill. Fast. I don't have time for this soul-mate, dramatic 'Fug', 'hel-lo', 'OMG', shit. And then we turn around and have a bunch of teenagers with special powers fucking up and apologizing and being forgiven when they really deserve to be smacked. ARGH, It's like House of Night all over again!<br /><br />And I get why Damen has such a large vocabulary, he's a million years old, but what the fuck? Ever is just like all the teens in the lame tv shows spouting dramatic, sappy lines and using words that only English majors use to impress drunk people at bars or high schoolers looking for a synonym to use in a paper because they already used everything else. Fuck this. I'm sick of books that make me feel stupid. This book was predictable and there are no resolutions! I feel like we just keep going in circles, Ever fucks up, hides it and Damen finds out, Damen tells her he loves her and will never leave her no matter how bad she fucks up, repeat. Ever is such a bitch. I hope she isn't a heroine. She' s a horrible role model.<br /><br />Haven. UGH. Haven was just a bitchy, selfish brat. Everything she did was expected and unfortunately not believable. Screw her. I hope I never meet someone in real life like her because I may have to punch them in the stomach.<br /><br />To be quite honest, the only one I didn't want to murder was Miles because he was gone most of the time. At least I think so, I skipped to the last chapter after 100 pages or so. Suffice to say I won't be revisiting this series again.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2532738441505966262" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mglVKg+EEu7gQsezSXVK3u8/zMRkwuEKnR8ecumgR/agLzz4tNrbhkdpc9K+gEABOWArDKpPb23GYVjDJOO1bA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CrTkBny+zOuBshHD523sQB2fIhjvII0up9HVzwOm31Awko3Ux+AFgyaZpaIQmOafy8DF0CGtA0n8r5N+zuUtyg==')})
  }

And she dared to defy Queen Tatiana, leader of the Moroi world, risking her life and reputation to protect generations of dhampir guardians to come.Now the law has finally caught up with Rose - for a crime she didn\'t even commit. She\'s in prison for the highest offense imaginable: the assassination of a monarch. She\'ll need help from both Dimitri and Adrian to find the one living person who can stall her execution and force the Moroi elite to acknowledge a shocking new candidate for the royal throne: Vasilisa Dragomir.But the clock on Rose\'s life is running out. Rose knows in her heart the world of the dead wants her back...and this time she is truly out of second chances. The big question is, when your whole life is about saving others, who will save you?Join Rose, Dimitri, Adrian, and Lissa in Last Sacrifice, the epic, unforgettable finale to Richelle Mead\'s international #1 bestselling Vampire Academy series.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"18381380517132830731\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n
